<DESCRIPTION>EX-99.1
<TEXT>
<HTML>
<HEAD>
<TITLE>exv99w1</TITLE>
</HEAD>
<BODY bgcolor="#FFFFFF">
<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<DIV style="font-family: Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif">


<DIV align="right" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 12pt"><b>Exhibit&nbsp;99.1</b>
</DIV>


<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 12pt"><B>Agria to Launch Partial Takeover Offer for PGG Wrightson Limited</B>
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt"><B>Beijing, China &#151; December&nbsp;23, 2010 &#151; </B>Agria Corporation (NYSE: GRO) (Agria) together
with China-based New Hope Group (New Hope) have today announced a partial takeover offer for PGG
Wrightson Limited (PGW).
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">The offer will be made by Agria (Singapore) Pte Ltd, which will be jointly owned, directly or
indirectly, by Agria and New Hope. Agria (Singapore), a wholly owned subsidiary of Agria
Corporation, currently holds a 19.01&nbsp;percent shareholding in PGW. The offer price will be NZ 60
cents per share for the purchase of 235.0&nbsp;million further shares in PGW. If the offer is
successful the resultant Agria (Singapore) shareholding in PGW will increase to 50.01&nbsp;percent.
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">The offer price of NZ 60 cents represents a 25% premium to today&#146;s closing price.
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Mr Xie Tao, CEO of Agria and current PGW director, said, &#147;This offer will provide existing PGW
shareholders an attractive opportunity and flexibility to sell a proportion of their shares at a
premium to the current market price and also allow them to retain an involvement to benefit from
the longer term opportunity Agria and New Hope will offer PGW. We are particularly keen to
strengthen the relationship between PGW and its key farmer customers and shareholders, who we see
as playing an increasingly important role in PGW in the future.&#148;
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">New Hope is one of China&#146;s largest agricultural and food corporations. The Group has revenue in
2010 of approximately RMB 60&nbsp;billion (equivalent to approximately NZ$12.1&nbsp;billion) and operates
throughout China, and in South-East Asia. New Hope Group has four large business units &#151;
agriculture and food (accounting for 85% of revenue), chemicals and resources, real-estate and
financial businesses.
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">New Hope&#146;s Chairman and founder, Mr Liu Yonghao, is a highly regarded businessman and is
Vice-Chairman of MinSheng Bank, one of China&#146;s largest commercial banks. Mr.&nbsp;Liu is also a member
of the Chinese People&#146;s Political Consultative Conference (CPPCC)&nbsp;economic committee.
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">New Hope Group is &#147;looking to strengthen its core focus with global partnerships, to contribute to
the bilateral agriculture partnership between China and New Zealand, and to contribute to the
future growth of New Zealand&#146;s agriculture industry.&#148;
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">New Hope will be Agria&#146;s investment partner and brings to bear a level of participation and reach
in the China agricultural sector that parallels PGW&#146;s involvement in the NZ industry. New Hope and
Agria have entered into a subscription agreement in respect of their ownership and participation in
Agria (Singapore).
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Mr Xie Tao further commented, &#147;PGW has underperformed expectations in recent times, including a
recent profit downgrade. In Agria&#146;s view, PGW&#146;s business requires restructuring and a refocus on
the core businesses of AgriServices and AgriTech to achieve its full potential. The proposed
transaction will provide PGW a committed cornerstone shareholder with the capacity to leverage
PGW&#146;s product and service offering to access opportunities in the China market for the benefit of
all PGW shareholders. This also introduces to PGW the financial capacity to refocus and
significantly grow the key PGW&#146;s businesses.&#148;
</DIV>





<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><!-- Folio -->&nbsp;<!-- /Folio -->
</DIV>

<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>

<DIV style="font-family: Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif">



<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">&#147;If this offer is successful PGW will remain as a NZ based listed company with a strong board led
by Chairman Sir John Anderson. I also look forward to working with the new managing director of PGW
following his appointment, which we understand is expected to be announced by PGW in the coming
days.&#148;
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">&#147;Agria has no intention to increase its shareholding above 50.01% if the offer is successful, and
has committed not to make a further offer at a higher price for a period of 12&nbsp;months.&#148;
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">A pre-bid agreement has been entered into with 18.3% shareholder Pyne Gould Corporation which has
committed to accept the partial offer in relation to all of its shareholding.
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">The offer
will allow PGW shareholders other than Agria to sell up to 38.3
percent of their holding
into the offer. Furthermore, shareholders can lodge additional acceptances for any further shares
they wish to sell. If the total number of shares tendered in the offer exceeds the 235.0&nbsp;million
being sought, then scaling will apply. The offer is conditional on
Agria obtaining a 50.01 percent shareholding and on relevant regulatory approvals including New Zealand Overseas Investment
Office and approval by the relevant authorities in China.
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">The takeover offer document is expected to be sent to all PGW shareholders in late January&nbsp;2011.
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Goldman Sachs &#038; Partners is acting as financial advisor to Agria and New Hope.
</DIV>


<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 12pt"><B>About Agria Corporation</B>
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Agria Corporation (NYSE: GRO) is a China-based company with investments in the agricultural sector.
For more information about Agria Corporation, please visit www.agriacorp.com.
</DIV>


<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 12pt"><B>Contacts:</B>
</DIV>

in Agria (Singapore).
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Mr Xie Tao further commented, &#147;PGW has underperformed expectations in recent times, including a
recent profit downgrade. In Agria&#146;s view, PGW&#146;s business requires restructuring and a refocus on
the core businesses of AgriServices and AgriTech to achieve its full potential. The proposed
transaction will provide PGW a committed cornerstone shareholder with the capacity to leverage
PGW&#146;s product and service offering to access opportunities in the China market for the benefit of
all PGW shareholders. This also introduces to PGW the financial capacity to refocus and
significantly grow the key PGW&#146;s businesses.&#148;
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">&#147;If this offer is successful PGW will remain as a NZ based listed company with a strong board led
by Chairman Sir John Anderson. I also look forward to working with the new
</DIV>






<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><!-- Folio -->&nbsp;<!-- /Folio -->
</DIV>

<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>

<DIV style="font-family: Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif">




<DIV align="right" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 12pt"><IMG src="h04714h0471410.gif" alt="(AGRIA LOGO)">
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">managing director of PGW following his appointment, which we understand is expected to be
announced by PGW in the coming days.&#148;
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">&#147;Agria has no intention to increase its shareholding above 50.01% if the offer is successful, and
has committed not to make a further offer at a higher price for a period of 12&nbsp;months.&#148;
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">A pre-bid agreement has been entered into with 18.3% shareholder Pyne Gould Corporation which has
committed to accept the partial offer in relation to all of its shareholding.
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">The offer will allow PGW shareholders other than Agria to sell up to 38.3 per cent of their
holding into the offer. Furthermore, shareholders can lodge additional acceptances for any further
shares they wish to sell. If the total number of shares tendered in the offer exceeds the 235.0
million being sought, then scaling will apply. The offer is conditional on Agria obtaining a 50.01
per cent shareholding and on relevant regulatory approvals including New Zealand Overseas
Investment Office and approval by the relevant authorities in China.
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">The takeover offer document is expected to be sent to all PGW shareholders in late January&nbsp;2011.
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Goldman Sachs &#038; Partners is acting as financial advisor to Agria and New Hope.
</DIV>


<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 12pt"><B>About Agria Corporation</B>
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Agria Corporation (NYSE: GRO) is a China-based company with investments in the agricultural sector.
For more information about Agria Corporation, please visit www.agriacorp.com.
</DIV>

</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt"><B>Background</B>
</DIV>


<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD align="left">A&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Agria Parent holds 100% of the shares in Agria bvi which holds 100% of the shares in Agria
Singapore (the 3 companies being referred to together as the <B>Agria Companies).</B></TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
<TD align="left">B&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Agria Singapore is the holder of 19.01% of the shares in PGG Wrightson Limited <B>(PGW) </B>and
Agria bvi is also the holder of convertible notes <B>(CRN) </B>issued by PGW.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
<TD align="left">C&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</TD>

    <TD>The Agria Companies and New Hope have agreed to cooperate to enable Agria Singapore to
make a partial takeover offer to purchase an additional 38.3% of the shares in PGW not already
held by Agria pursuant to the New Zealand Takeovers Code in the event the parties agree to
proceed to make a takeover offer.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">


<TD align="left">D&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>In this event Agria Parent and New Hope have agreed between themselves and with the other
Agria Companies to make the funds available to complete the purchase of shares in PGW
pursuant to a takeover offer as provided in this Agreement.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>
</DIV>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left"><B>3.</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><B>Obligation to fund the takeover</B></TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Agria Parent and New Hope jointly and severally covenant with Agria bvi and Agria Singapore
that forthwith upon the Takeover Offer becoming unconditional, and prior to the date upon which
Agria Singapore makes payment for shares in PGW to be acquired pursuant to the Takeover Offer, they
will ensure that Agria Singapore is put in funds by way of Agria Parent and New Hope directly, or
indirectly through Agria bvi or another company in the Agria group of companies, subscribing and
paying for shares in Agria Singapore, which subscription may be made in conjunction with other
funding arrangements agreed by Agria Singapore, to enable Agria Singapore to meet its obligations
under the Takeover Offer, it being acknowledged that the obligation of Agria Singapore to complete
the purchase of shares in PGW pursuant to the Takeover Offer is subject to the terms and conditions
of the Takeover Offer including the requirement to obtain regulatory consents in New Zealand and
China. It is acknowledged and agreed that New Hope will be entitled to procure an associated
company of New Hope to perform the obligations of New Hope under this Agreement.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">

faith in order to agree and implement a fair and equitable arrangement under which Agria bvi and
Agria Singapore will be funded <B>(Funding Arrangement) </B>so as to satisfy the funding obligations of
Agria Parent and New Hope under clause 3.</TD>
</TR>

<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">

    <TD>all necessary consents being obtained, including:</TD>

<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

    <TD>under the Overseas Investment Act 2005;</TD>

<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>

</TR>

<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>

    <TD>if sent by facsimile, on the date and time shown on the transmission report by the
machine from which the facsimile was sent which indicates that the facsimile was sent in its
entirety and in legible form to the facsimile number of the addressee notified for the purposes of
this clause but if the delivery, receipt or transmission is on a day which is not a Business Day or
is after 5.00 p.m. (addressee&#146;s time), it is deemed to have been received at 9.00 a.m. on the next
Business Day; or</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="4%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(d)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>if sent by email, on the date and time at which it enters the addressee&#146;s information
system (as shown in a confirmation of delivery report from the sender&#146;s information system, which
indicates that email was sent to the email address of the addressee notified for the purposes of
this clause), but if the delivery, receipt or transmission is on a day which is not a Business Day
or is after 5.00 p.m. (addressee&#146;s time), it is deemed to have been received at 9.00 a.m. on the
next Business Day.</TD>

    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Except where this Agreement expressly states otherwise, this Agreement does not create a
relationship of employment, trust, agency or partnership between the parties.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>

    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">2.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Offer</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left"><B>2.1</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><B>Offer</B></TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Subject to clause 2.5, the Purchaser shall make a takeover offer for the acquisition of
38.3% of the shares in the Company (234,963,939 shares) not currently held by the Purchaser
and which taken together with the shares in the Company that the Purchaser already owns will
result in the Purchaser acquiring 50.01% of the shares in the Company, under rule 41 of the
Takeovers Code at a price of not less than $0.60 per share and substantially on the terms
and conditions set out in the Draft Offer Document, which shall comply with the Takeovers
Code.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left"><B>2.2</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><B>Variations to the Offer Document</B></TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The Vendor acknowledges that the Draft Offer Document is not in final form and may be
amended by the Purchaser prior to the offer being made, provided that no such amendment
materially and detrimentally affects the rights or obligations of the Vendor as set out in
the Draft Offer Document which shall be deemed to include any materially adverse amendments
to the terms of any of the conditions to the Draft Offer Document and the latest date that
the Purchaser can declare the Offer unconditional, being 15 April&nbsp;2011, set out in
paragraphs 3.5 and 4.1 of the Draft Offer Document (unless the Vendor agrees to such
amendments in writing) and for the avoidance of doubt no change can be made to reduce the
Offer price.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left"><B>2.3</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><B>Date of Offer</B></TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">

    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Notwithstanding any other provision in this deed, the Purchaser will be entitled to
nominate a subsidiary to be the offeror under the Offer in which case such nominee will be
considered to be the Purchaser (with all the rights and obligations of the Purchaser) under
this deed. Notwithstanding such nomination, Agria (Singapore) Pte Ltd. will remain liable to
the Vendor for all of the Purchaser&#146;s obligations under this deed and any breach by the
Purchaser of its obligations under this deed.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">7.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>General</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left"><B>7.1</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><B>Entire agreement</B></TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>This deed constitutes the entire agreement between the parties in connection with
its subject matter and supersedes all previous agreements or understandings between the
parties in connection with its subject matter.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left"><B>7.2</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><B>Further action</B></TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Each party must do, at its own expense, everything reasonably necessary (including
executing documents) to give full effect to this deed and the transactions contemplated by
it.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left"><B>7.3</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><B>Severability</B></TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>A term or part of a term of this deed that is illegal or unenforceable may be severed
from this deed and the remaining terms or part of a term of this deed continue in force.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left"><B>7.4</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><B>Waiver</B></TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>A party does not waive a right, power or remedy if it fails to exercise or delays in
exercising the right, power or remedy. A single or partial exercise by a party of a right,
power or remedy does not prevent another or further exercise of that or another right, power
or remedy. A waiver of a right, power or remedy must be in writing and signed by the party
giving the waiver.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left"><B>7.5</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><B>No agency</B></TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Nothing contained in this deed is deemed to constitute any of the parties the agent or
legal representative of any other party except as otherwise expressly provided in this deed.
No party has
authority to assume any obligation or liability on behalf of the other party.</TD>
</TR>



</TABLE>

<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>

<DIV style="font-family: Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif">


<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt"><TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">


<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left"><B>7.6</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><B>Counterparts</B></TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>This deed can be signed in one or more counterparts (including facsimile copies), each of
which is deemed to be an original but all of which together will constitute only one and the
same deed.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left"><B>7.7</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><B>Notices:</B></TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>
</DIV>

<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="4%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(a)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>All notices, requests, demands and other communications shall be in writing and
shall be deemed to have been duly given if delivered in person, posted or sent by
facsimile or email to the party concerned at its physical address, email address or
facsimile number as set out below or to such other address or number as it shall advise
to the other party in writing.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="4%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(b)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>A letter shall be deemed to have been given or sent the day after being
deposited in the post.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="4%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(c)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>A notice, request demand or other communication sent by:</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>
</DIV>

<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="8%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(i)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>delivered by hand, shall be deemed served when
left at the address of the addressee;</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="8%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(ii)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>if sent by pre-paid post, three Business Days (if posted
within New Zealand to an address in New Zealand) or five Business Days (if
posted by airmail from one country to another) after the date of posting;</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="8%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(iii)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>sent by facsimile (provided the sending facsimile machine
produces a print-out of the time, date and uninterrupted transmission of the
message) shall be deemed served immediately upon completion of sending;</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="8%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(iv)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>sent by email, shall be deemed served on the date and time
at which it enters the addressee&#146;s information system unless a delivery failure
notice has been received by the send, in which case the notice will be deemed
not to have been served,</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>
</DIV>

<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="4%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>provided that if a notice is received or deemed to be received on a on a day which is
not a Business Day, or is received or deemed to be received after 5.00pm on a
Business Day, in the place where the addressee is based, that notice will be deemed
to have been received by the recipient at 9.00am on the next Business Day.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>
</DIV>

<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>
<DIV style="font-family: Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif">


<DIV align="center" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 18pt"><B>PARTIAL TAKEOVER OFFER BY</B>
</DIV>


<DIV align="Center" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt"><B>Agria (Singapore) Pte Ltd.</B>
</DIV>

<DIV align="Center" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt"><B>to purchase an additional 38.3% of the shares in</B>
</DIV>

<DIV align="Center" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt"><B>PGG Wrightson Limited not currently held by Agria (Singapore) Pte Ltd.</B>
</DIV>

<DIV align="Center" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt"><B>at NZ$0.60 per share <BR><BR style="font-size: 6pt">
made pursuant to the Takeovers Code</B>
</DIV>

<DIV align="Center" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">To accept this Offer see page 2
</DIV>

<DIV align="center" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 18pt"><B>IMPORTANT</B>
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt"><B>IF YOU ARE IN DOUBT AS TO ANY ASPECT OF THIS OFFER, YOU SHOULD CONSULT YOUR FINANCIAL OR LEGAL
ADVISOR.</B>
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt"><B>IF YOU HAVE SOLD ALL YOUR SHARES IN PGG WRIGHTSON LIMITED TO WHICH THIS OFFER APPLIES, YOU SHOULD
IMMEDIATELY HAND THIS OFFER DOCUMENT AND THE ACCOMPANYING ACCEPTANCE FORM TO THE PURCHASER, OR THE
AGENT (EG THE BROKER) THROUGH WHOM THE SALE WAS MADE, TO BE PASSED TO THE PURCHASER.</B>
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt"><B>PGG WRIGHTSON LIMITED&#146;S TARGET COMPANY STATEMENT, TOGETHER WITH AN INDEPENDENT ADVISER&#146;S REPORT ON
THE MERITS OF THIS OFFER EITHER ACCOMPANIES THIS OFFER OR WILL BE SENT TO YOU &#091;WITHIN 14 DAYS&#093; AND
SHOULD BE READ IN CONJUNCTION WITH THIS OFFER.</B>
</DIV>


<DIV align="Center" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt"><B>THIS IS AN IMPORTANT DOCUMENT AND REQUIRES YOUR IMMEDIATE <BR>
ATTENTION</B>
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 12pt">2077929:SYS</DIV>
<DIV align="right" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: -12pt"><!-- Folio -->1<!-- /Folio -->
</DIV></DIV>

<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>

<DIV style="font-family: Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif">

<DIV align="center" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 18pt"><B>SUMMARY OF OFFER</B>
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">On 23 December&nbsp;2010 <B>Agria (Singapore) Pte Ltd. </B>(<B>Agria</B>) announced that it would make a partial
takeover offer for an additional 38.3% of the shares in PGG Wrightson Limited (<B>PGW</B>) that it does
not already hold, which if successful, will bring Agria&#146;s total shareholding in PGW (once the offer
is declared unconditional and the relevant shares are transferred) to 50.01%. The key terms of the
offer are:
</DIV>


<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left"><FONT style="font-family: Wingdings">&#216;</FONT></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Consideration of NZ$0.60 per share in PGW.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left"><FONT style="font-family: Wingdings">&#216;</FONT></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Offer closes 5 p.m. on &#091;15 April&nbsp;2011&#093; (unless extended).</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left"><FONT style="font-family: Wingdings">&#216;</FONT></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The offer is conditional. The conditions of the Offer are set out on paragraphs 0 and 4 of
this document.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>
</DIV>

<DIV align="center" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 18pt"><B>HOW TO ACCEPT THIS OFFER</B>
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">To accept the offer by Agria, you should complete the Acceptance Form enclosed with this document,
in accordance with the instructions set out on the Acceptance Form, as soon as possible. Then
deliver, mail or fax the Acceptance Form to:
</DIV>


<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">&#091;Computershare Investor Services Limited<BR>
Re: &#091;Agria (Singapore) Pte Ltd.&#093;<BR>
Private Bag 92119<BR>
Auckland 1142<BR>
159 Hurstmere Road, Takapuna, North Shore City 0622<BR>
Facsimile: &#043;64 9 488 8787&#093;

</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">You may accept the offer in respect of all or any of your shares. If you have sold all or some of
your shares, please refer to the instructions on page &#091;17&#093; of this document.
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Acceptances must be received by Agria by 5pm on &#091;15 April&nbsp;2011&#093;.
</DIV>

<DIV style="font-family: Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif">




<DIV align="center" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 18pt"><B>TERMS AND CONDITIONS OF PARTIAL TAKEOVER OFFER<BR>
BY AGRIA (SINGAPORE)&nbsp;PTE LTD. TO PURCHASE<BR>
AN ADDITIONAL 38.3% OF THE SHARES IN PGG WRIGHTSON LIMITED<BR>
NOT ALREADY HELD BY AGRIA (SINGAPORE)&nbsp;PTE LTD.</B>
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Dear Shareholder,
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Agria (Singapore) Pte Ltd. (<B>Agria</B>) hereby offers to acquire, on the terms and conditions set out in
this document (the <B>Offer</B>), an additional 38.3% (the <B>Specified Percentage</B>) of the issued fully paid
ordinary shares in PGG Wrightson Limited (<B>PGW</B>) not currently held by Agria, and which would (once
the Offer is declared unconditional and the relevant shares are transferred) bring Agria&#146;s total
shareholding in PGW to 50.01%. All the shares in PGW are referred to in this Offer as the <B>Shares</B>
and each of them is referred to as a <B>Share</B>.
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">This Offer is a partial offer for the Shares. As Agria holds 144,104,680 Shares, the Offer is for
the Specified Percentage of the Shares, which are not already held by Agria at the date of this
Offer. In accordance with the Takeovers Code, each holder of Shares is entitled to sell to Agria
pursuant to the Offer, the Specified Percentage of the Shares they hold (<B>Entitlement</B>).
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Agria Corporation (the parent company of Agria), Agria and New Hope Group have entered into a
Subscription Agreement whereunder Agria Corporation and New Hope Group jointly and severally
covenant to subscribe for shares in Agria, either directly or indirectly through another company in
the Agria group, and provide other funding support as agreed with Agria, to ensure that Agria is
put in funds to enable it to meet its obligations under the Takeover Offer. Accordingly, if the
Offer becomes unconditional, Agria Corporation and New Hope Group will be the shareholders,
directly or indirectly, of Agria prior to payment by Agria of any consideration payable for the
Shares of acceptors under the Offer.
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">To the extent holders of Shares do not accept the Offer for their full Entitlement, Agria is
entitled to accept acceptances from holders of Shares who wish to sell more Shares than their
Entitlement. Over-acceptances of this Offer will be dealt with as set out in paragraph 2 below.
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">This Offer is made subject to the following terms and conditions.
</DIV>

debentures or convertible notes or voting securities or grants any other rights or interests
in its shares to its shareholders by way of capitalisation of any part of its profits or
reserves, unless paragraph 4.2(b) is waived by Agria, Acceptors of this Offer will be bound to
transfer such shares or debentures or convertible notes or other rights and interests to
Agria, without any additional consideration.</TD>

after 23 December&nbsp;2010 then this Offer will be interpreted to take into account such
consolidation, subdivision or acquisition and will be deemed to be for the shares/securities
resulting from such consolidation, subdivision or acquisition and the consideration per Share
provided for under paragraph 1.1 will be increased or reduced, as the case may require, in
proportion to such consolidation, subdivision or acquisition, and Acceptors will be bound to
transfer such consolidated, subdivided or acquired shares to Agria on the basis of the
consideration so increased or reduced.</TD>
</TR>

provided in paragraph 1.1 above.</TD>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 12pt"><B>NOTES AND INSTRUCTIONS FOR COMPLETION</B>
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">1 <B>INTERPRETATION</B>: In this form references to the Transferor in the singular shall include the plural.
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">2 <B>TO ACCEPT THE OFFER</B>: Sign this form where marked &#147;Signed by the Transferor(s)&#148; and have your signature witnessed. Any person
(including your husband or wife) may witness your signature and must add his or her occupation
and full address in the space
provided.
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Companies must sign in accordance with the Companies Act 1993.
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">3 METHOD OF PAYMENT: You should select a Method of Payment. If you do not, or the details
that you provide are not sufficient to effect an electronic transfer to you, you will be
paid by cheque or by Direct Credit to your existing nominated account held in
Computershare&#146;s registers.
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">4 <B>JOINT HOLDERS</B>: If the shares are registered in the names of joint holders, all must sign the
form.
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">5 <B>POWER OF ATTORNEY</B>: If the form is signed under a power of attorney, the relevant power of
attorney and a certificate of non-revocation must be submitted with the form for noting and
return, and the certificate printed overleaf must be completed. Where such power of attorney
has already been noted by PGW, then this fact must be stated under the signature of the
attorney.
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt"><U>6 <B>ON COMPLETION</B>: Place the signed form in the enclosed reply paid envelope and
post or fax to the Transferee on:</U><BR>
&#091;Computershare Investor Services Limited
</DIV>


<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 0pt">Re: &#091;Agria (Singapore) Pte Ltd.&#093;<BR>
Private Bag 92119<BR>
Auckland 1142<BR>
159 Hurstmere Road, Takapuna, North Shore City 0622

</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">You can also fax this Acceptance Form to Computershare Investor Services Limited on &#043;64 9 488
8787. If you do that, the original form should also be delivered or posted to the above address (although failure to do
that will not invalidate your acceptance). Please mark the original form clearly &#147;FAXED&#148;.<BR>
<u>as soon as possible, but in any event so as to be received not
later than &#091;5pm on 15 April&nbsp;2011&#093; (subject to the Offer).</u>
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">7 <B>PREVIOUS SALE</B>: If you have sold all your shares, please pass this form together with the offer documents to your
sharebroker or the purchasers of such shares. If you have sold part of your shareholding,
record that fact on this form by
amending the number of shares noted as being held by you on the face of this form.

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Agria (Singapore) Pte Ltd. <B>(Agria), </B>the holder of 19.01% of PGG Wrightson Limited, hereby
gives notice pursuant to Rule&nbsp;41(1) of the Takeovers Code of its intention to make a partial offer
under the Takeovers Code to acquire an additional 38.3% of the issued ordinary shares in PGG
Wrightson Limited <B>(Offer) </B>not currently held by it.
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">The proposed Offer consideration will be NZ$0.60 per share.
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Attached to this notice are the intended terms of the Offer, including the information required by
Schedule&nbsp;1 of the Takeovers Code, stated as at the date of this notice. The Offer will be made in
the form attached with any modifications and additional information permitted or required to be
contained in, or to accompany, this notice.
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">This notice is dated 23 December&nbsp;2010.
</DIV>
